)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF DATA CARDS FOLLOWCV
)@@G@@ THE CONTROL CARD, THEY ARE            *******  @H@@@@. ******* ASSUMED CW
)@@G@@TO BE PARTIAL SGS STATEMENTS WHICH ARE             *******  @H@@@@. ****CX
)@@G@@*** TO BE COMPLETED.  AFTER ALL THE CARDS ARE READ,            *******  CY

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF 'C' OPTION ON) AS A QUESTION.  THE USER (DA
)@@G@@OR             *******  @H@@@@. ******* OPERATOR) RESPONSE COMPLETES THEDB
)@@G@@ SGS IMAGE WHICH           *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS THEN WRITTEN TO TDC
)@@G@@HE OUTPUT ELEMENT.  SEVERAL            *******  @H@@@@. ******* CONTROL DD

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* *ELSE                       -   GENERATION  DH
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@@. ******* *END                            DI
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DJ

)@@G@@***                             -   RESPONSE IS 'YES' OR 'Y'   *******  DM
)@@G@@@H@@@@. ******* *REPEAT LAST                - REPEAT LAST SGS           DN
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* *FILE                       - A MODE 4 TYPE DO
)@@G@@FILE SGS IS    *******  @H@@@@. *******                             -   DP
)@@G@@GENERATED FROM NEXT INPUT  *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DQ
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF A '*RDR
)@@G@@EPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN '*IF LAST ....' STATEMENT,  *******  @H@@@@. ****DS
)@@G@@*** THE STATEMENT BEFORE THE '*IF' STATEMENT IS REPEATED UNTIL *******  DT
)@@G@@@H@@@@. ******* THE CONDITION ON THE '*IF' STATEMENT BECOMES TRUE.      DU
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF A '*REPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN SGS IMAGE, THDV
)@@G@@AT SGS IMAGE   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS REPEATED UNTIL A RESPONSE OF DW
)@@G@@'$END' IS GIVEN.           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DX
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@@. ******* AN ANSWEDY
)@@G@@R OF '$SKIP' TO ANY SGS QUESTION, WILL SKIP        *******  @H@@@@. ****DZ

)@@G@@PUT ELEMENT WITH NO        *******  @H@@@@. ******* FURTHER ACTION.     EE

)@@G@@LLOW THE FIRST (WITH A @EOF*******  @H@@@@. ******* IN BETWEEN), THEY WIEL

)@@G@@TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********                                KS
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@Q. ******** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    =KT

)@@G@@  . READ NEXT STRING    @D@@@!          L,U       A3,0,A0           . WOQA
)@@G@@RD COUNT    @ @@@!          LXI       A0,A3     @ @@@!          LXM,U   QB

)@@G@@HE *******  @H@@@Q. ******** EXEC 8.  THESE PROCS ARE MADE AVAILABLE TO FV

)@@G@@F THIS ELEMENT HAS NOT BEEN*******  @H@@@Q. ******** INCORPORATED INTO TFX
)@@G@@HE OPERATING SYSTEM, IT FIRST MUST BE  *******  @H@@@Q. ******** PDP'ED FY
)@@G@@INTO THE FILE FROM WHICH THE CALLING PROGRAM IS    *******  @H@@@Q. ****FZ
)@@G@@**** BEING ASSEMBLED.                                          *******  GA

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************************GC
)@@G@@**********************  @D@@@QLIPROC$*  $PROC     0                 . MAGD
)@@G@@STER PROC   @D@@@QLIPROCS*  $NAME                       . ALTERNATE NAMEGE
)@@G@@@H@T@Q          AXR$                        . STANDARD ASSEMBLER REGISTEGF
)@@G@@R NAMES     @H@@@T          $INCLUDE  'MAXR$/'          . STANDARD ASSEMGG
)@@G@@BLER REGISTER NAMES     @H@@@Q. ****************************************GH
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@Q. ******** CHECK XQT OPTION $PGI
)@@G@@ROC- ISOLATES BIT CORR. TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********        GJ
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@Q. ****GK
)@@G@@**** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  GL
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********       TOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)              GM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)  GN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000GO
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SOPT 'U'    =GP
)@@G@@ TOP A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SGQ
)@@G@@OPT A2,'U' = TOP A2,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****GR
)@@G@@****       GOPT 'U'    = ER OPT$                               *******  GS
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                     AND A0,(000000000040)              GT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************************GU
)@@G@@**********************  @#@@@QP         $PROC   @^@@@QTOPT**    $NAME   GV
)@@G@@  0   @^@@@QAOPT**    $NAME     0   @^@@@QGOPT**    $NAME     1   @^@@@QGW
)@@G@@SOPT**    $NAME     2   @A@@@Q          $DO P(0,0)=1 , ER OPT$    @F@@@QGX
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)<2)**(P(1)=1) , AND A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@QGY
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=0)**(P(1)>1) , AND P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @F@@@QGZ
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)=1) , TOP A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@QHA
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)>1) , TOP P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @#@@@QHB
)@@G@@          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********************************HC
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@Q. ******** FORTRAN CALL HD
)@@G@@$PROC                                        *******  @H@@@Q. ********  HE
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@QHF
)@@G@@. ******** CALL SUBR A,B,C,D  = LMJ X11,SUBR                         ***HG
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********                      + A                         HH
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********                      + B             HI
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                      + C HJ
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********              HK
)@@G@@        + D                                  *******  @H@@@Q. ********  HL
)@@G@@                    + 0                                  *******  @H@@@QHM

)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. ****************************HQ
)@@G@@**********************************************  @H@@@Q. ******** INFOR THR
)@@G@@ABLE INTERFACE PROCS - AIDS IN USING RINF$, SELT$  *******  @H@@@Q. ****HS
)@@G@@****               AND DUSE$ SUBROUTINES                       *******  HT

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ******** R$INF - CALLS 'RINF$' AND INVOKES 'ELT$'   HV
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$ELT - CALLS 'SELT$' WITH PARAHW
)@@G@@METER #                    *******  @H@@@Q. ******** D$USE - CALLS 'DUSEHX
)@@G@@$' WITH FILE$NAME(MAY BE R.J.)         *******  @H@@@Q. ****************HY
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@QP     HZ
)@@G@@    $PROC     1    . A PARAMETER SPECIFIES # OF XQT PARAMETERS EXPECTED,IA
)@@G@@@D@@@QR$INF**   $NAME          .      OTHERWISE 3 ASSUMED   @F@@@Q      IB
)@@G@@    $LEVEL    0,1,0             . MAKE ELT$ LABELS GLOBAL   @E@@@Q      IC
)@@G@@    ELT$                        . INVOKE 'ELT$' PROC  @F@@@Q          $LID
)@@G@@EVEL    0,0,0             . RETURN TO NORMAL LEVELING @B@@@QNN        $EIE
)@@G@@QU      28*(3*(P=1)+P(1,1))   @A@@@Q          L         A0,(NN,INF)     IF
)@@G@@@ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,RINF$ @^@@@Q          J         ERR @^@@@QIG
)@@G@@          J         CONT@^@@@QINF       RES       NN  @ @@@QERR       ERIH
)@@G@@        PRINT$    @ @@@Q          ER        EXIT$     @]@@@QCONT      . II
)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$ELT**   $NIJ
)@@G@@AME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , L,U A0,P(1,1)@^@@@Q          LMJ X11,IK
)@@G@@SELT$ @#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QD$USE*IL
)@@G@@*   $NAME   @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , DL A0,($CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @ @@@QIM
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,DUSE$ @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@QIN
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************IO
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ******** SOURCE OUTPUT PROCS - AIDS IN USING SSOR, SOR, ANIP
)@@G@@D ESOR   *******  @H@@@Q. ********                       SUBROUTINES    IQ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                          IR
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$SOR - SETS IS
)@@G@@UP 'PARTBL', ASSIGNS FILE AND CALLS 'SSOR'   *******  @H@@@Q. ********  IT
)@@G@@       P(1,1) =   FILE $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)                *******  @H@@@QIU
)@@G@@. ********         P(1,2) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               ***IV
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,3) = VERSION $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)      IW
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(0,1) = 1, IF NOT FIRST TIMEIX
)@@G@@ CALLED              *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$OR  - CALLS 'SOR'      IY
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1IZ
)@@G@@) = (NWDS,ADDR)                              *******  @H@@@Q. ********  JA
)@@G@@       P(1,1),P(1,2) = ADDR,NWDS                         *******  @H@@@QJB
)@@G@@. ******** E$SOR - CALLS 'ESOR'                                      ***JC
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. **********************************************************JD
)@@G@@****************  @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$SOR**   $NAME   JE
)@@G@@@A@@@Q          $DO P(0,1)=0 , GO CONT1   @B@@@Q          DL        A0,(JF
)@@G@@$CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PARTBL+27    @B@@@Q      JG
)@@G@@    DL        A0,($CFS(P(1,2)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PARTBL+JH
)@@G@@29    @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)>2 , DL A0,($CFS(P(1,3)DL))   @B@@@Q      JI
)@@G@@    $DO P(1)>2 , DS A0,PARTBL+33    @#@@@QCONT1     $NAME   @A@@@Q      JJ
)@@G@@    L         A0,(3,PARTBL+26)@^@@@Q          ER        CSF$@ @@@Q      JK
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,SSOR$ @^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@ @@@Q          $DJL
)@@G@@O P(0,1) , $END   @^@@@Q          J         CONT@^@@@QPARTBL**  RES     JM
)@@G@@  26  @#@@@Q          '@ASG'  @^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1,1)DL)@^@@@Q      JN
)@@G@@    $CFS(P(1,2)DL)@^@@@Q          RES       2   @^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1JO
)@@G@@,3)DL)@^@@@Q          RES       8   @]@@@QCONT      . @#@@@Q          $EJP
)@@G@@ND    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$OR**    $NAME   @A@@@Q      JQ
)@@G@@    $DO P(1)=1 , L A0,P(1,1)  @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)=2 , L A0,(P(1,2),JR
)@@G@@P(1,1))     @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,SOR$  @^@@@Q          ER      JS
)@@G@@  ERR$@#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QE$SOR**   $PROC     0   @ @@@Q      JT
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,ESOR$ @^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@#@@@Q          $EJU
)@@G@@ND    @H@@@Q. **********************************************************JV
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@Q. ******* TEST FACILITY FOR MASM ELEMENTS       JW
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. *******                           JX
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ******* IF @MASM,T USEJY
)@@G@@D, FACILITY IS PROCED ON AND IF T2 OF        *******  @H@@@Q. ******* RUJZ
)@@G@@N CONDITION WORD IS = 2 (@SETC 2), SNOOPY IS TURNED ON   *******  @H@@@QKA
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***KB
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. **********************************************************KC
)@@G@@****************  @#@@@QTEST**    $PROC   @G@@@QMASMT*    $EQU      $PARKD
)@@G@@(0)**(1*/('Z'-'T')) . TEST MODE IF @MASM,T USED @C@@@RLCN       $EQU    KE
)@@G@@  $LCN              . SAVE LC @ @@@Q          $IF       MASMT     @G@@@QKF
)@@G@@          J         CONT1             . JUMP TO ANOTHER LOCATION COUNTERKG
)@@G@@@B@@@R$(0)      '*TEST*'  . FOR IDONLY$ USE     @]@R@Q$($LCN+2)   @]@@@RKH
)@@G@@$(LCN+2)    @^@@@QSAVE      $RES      2   @D@@@QCONT1     DS        A0,SKI
)@@G@@AVE           . SAVE A0,A1    @E@@@Q          COND$                     KJ
)@@G@@  . GET CONDITION WORD  @D@@@Q          AND       A0,(0770000)      . ISKK
)@@G@@OLATE T2    @F@@@Q          TNE       A1,(020000)       . IF = 2, TURN OKL
)@@G@@N SNOOPY    @^@@@Q          SLJ       TON$@D@@@Q          DL        A0,SKM
)@@G@@AVE           . RESTORE A0,A1 @H@@@Q          J         CONT2           KN
)@@G@@  . JUMP BACK TO ORIGINAL LOCATION COUNTER@#@R@Q$($LCN-2),CONT2   @#@T@RKO
)@@G@@$(LCN-2),CONT2    @]@@@T$(LCN),CONT2@#@@@R          $ELSE   @#@@@R$(0)  KP

)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    _@@@@@(1,1)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PKR

)@@G@@    $LEVEL    0,1,0     @^@@@@P         $PROC     *1  @ @@@@FORK$*    $NKU

)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. ******* THE 'BYTESUB' SUBROUTINES ARE RERC
)@@G@@FERENCED.                  *******  @H@@@9. *******                     RD
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* REVISIONRE
)@@G@@ SUMMARY                                           *******  @H@@@8. ****RF
)@@G@@*** ----------------                                           *******  RG
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         RH
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R1  - FIRST RELEASE                        RI
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R2  - REMOVE TAPE LOGIC AND REPRJ
)@@G@@LACE WITH                  *******  @H@@@8. *******      - CHECK FOR PRERK
)@@G@@-ASSIGNED LOG FILES                    *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R3  - ARL
)@@G@@SSUME BLOCKS SPAN LESS THAN 1 HOUR OF DATA         *******  @H@@@8. ****RM
)@@G@@***      - SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO ENTRIES                         *******  RN
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******      - ALLOW MULTI-REEL LOG TAPES                       RO
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******      - SIGNAL CALLING PROG WHEN NEW BLOCK RERP
)@@G@@AD             *******  @H@@@8. *******      - DON'T LEAVE ANY MASS STORRQ
)@@G@@AGE LOG FILES ASSIGNED     *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R4  - SKIP EXEC 8 ERR
)@@G@@NTRIES UNLESS PRIVILEGED               *******  @H@@@9. *******      - ARS
)@@G@@SSEMBLE WITH MASM                                  *******  @H@@@9. ****RT
)@@G@@*** 1R5  - CHECK FOR AN ALTERNATE LOG FILE CALLED 'LOG$'       *******  RU
)@@G@@@H@@@9. *******      - CALCULATE SECTOR ADDRESS OF 1ST BLOCK TO ALLOW   RV
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. *******        FOR FILES COPIED FROM TAPE           RW
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. *******      - ASSIGN SYSTEM LOG FILES WRX
)@@G@@ITH 'I' OPTION             *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R6  - FIX LOGIC FORRY
)@@G@@ SEARCH KEY OPTION                     *******  @H@@@9. *******      - ARZ
)@@G@@DD 'L' OPTION SUMMARY                              *******  @H@@@9. ****SA
)@@G@@***      - ADD STRING SCAN FEATURE                             *******  SB
)@@G@@@H@@@9. *******      - CALCULATE 1ST CYCLE OF LOG FILE                  SC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R7  - EXTERNALIZE TAG 'ENTRYNUM' FOR SKIPPISD
)@@G@@NG BLOCK       *******  @H@@@9. *******      - EXTERNALIZE TAG 'PRINTCYCSE
)@@G@@LE' FOR CYCLE SUMMARY      *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R8  - ADD EXTERNAL SF
)@@G@@CELLS 'NBLOCKS' & 'NRECS'              *******  @H@@@9. *******      - USG
)@@G@@SE 1180 INSTRUCTIONS                               *******  @H@@@9. ****SH
)@@G@@*** 1R9  - FIX LATEST CYCLE BUG                                *******  SI
)@@G@@@H@@@'. ******* 1R10 - ADD LOOK AHEAD CYCLE FEATURE                     SJ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******                                             SK
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************SL
)@@G@@**********************************  @#@9@8          AXR$    @]@9@8$(1),RSM
)@@G@@EADLG*@#@@@9$(1),READLG* AXR$ @H@@@8          L         X10,X11         SN
)@@G@@  . GET PARAMETER TABLE (IN X11 IF FOR V  @E@@@8          TZ,S1     0,X1SO
)@@G@@1             .   , IN A0 IF FTN)   @ @@@8          L         X10,A0    SP
)@@G@@@^@@@8          SZ        BUFF@ @@@8          L         X5,POINTER@E@@@8SQ
)@@G@@          TZ        FIRST             . FIRST TIME ENTERED? @B@9@8      SR
)@@G@@    J         CONT1             . NO@B@@@9          J         CONT2     SS
)@@G@@        . NO@F@9@8          S         X10,FIRST         . YES, SET FIRSTST
)@@G@@ TIME KEY   @F@@@9          SP1       FIRST             . YES, SET FIRSTSU
)@@G@@ TIME KEY   @E@@@9          PCT$      BUFFER,5          . GET PART OF PCSV
)@@G@@T     @F@@@9          L,S2      A0,BUFFER+4       . IF RUN PRIVILEGED, SSW
)@@G@@ET KEY@ @@@9          TEP,U     A0,040    @^@@@9          SP1       PRIVSX
)@@G@@@G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE1         . '@USE MASTER,SYS$*SYSTEM$LSY
)@@G@@OG$'  @H@@@8          FACIL$    FACPKT            . IS THERE A LOG FILE SZ
)@@G@@ASSIGNED ALREADY? @F@@@8          TNZ,S1    FACPKT+6          . IF FILE TA
)@@G@@NOT PRE-ASSIGNED, @H@9@8          J         CONT0             .     GO TTB
)@@G@@O REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@/@9          J         CONT0           TC
)@@G@@  .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@@@/          J         CONTTD
)@@G@@1             .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @F@9@8          S TE
)@@G@@        A0,PREASG         . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SET KEY@F@@@9          SPTF
)@@G@@1       PREASG            . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SET KEY@F@9@8          J TG
)@@G@@        CONT1             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @F@@@9          J TH
)@@G@@        CONT2             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @E@;@9CONT0     E$TI
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@;@9          E$MSG   TJ
)@@G@@  USE @D@;@9          E$DECV    0,,U              . PRESENT CYCLE @#@;@9TK
)@@G@@          E$MSGR  @G@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . '@USE LOTL
)@@G@@G$,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$(0)' @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . '@TM
)@@G@@ASG,AI LOG$'@F@/@;CONT0     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST TN
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @F@@@/CONT1     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST TO
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @ @@@;          L,U       A6,' '    @ @@@;          SLJ     TP
)@@G@@  CYCLE     @D@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT          . GET LEAD ITEM TQ
)@@G@@@H@@@9                                      . CHANGE MSCON PKT TO READ MTR
)@@G@@AIN ITEM    @E@@@9          SP1,S3    MSCONPKT+3        .   FOR LATER CATS
)@@G@@LLS   @G@@@9          L,S4      A0,BUFFER+9       . CALCULATE OLDEST RELTT
)@@G@@ CYCLE-1    @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@C@@@9          SN        A0,LTU
)@@G@@OGCYCLE       . STORE   @E@9@8CONT0     LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GETV
)@@G@@T NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@/@9CONT1     LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXTTW
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@/          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CTX
)@@G@@YCLE  @C@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR   @F@9@8CONT1 TY
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,READ          . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@9CONT2 TZ
)@@G@@    LMJ       X9,READ           . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@8      UA
)@@G@@    L         A0,0,X5           . CHECK FOR END OF CYCLE    @ @@@8      UB
)@@G@@    TNE       A0,(-0)   @C@9@8          J         CONT7             . YEUC
)@@G@@S     @C@@@9          J         CONT11            . YES     @H@@@8      UD
)@@G@@    TE        A0,SENTINEL       . CHECK FOR LAST TAPE BLOCK SENTINEL    UE
)@@G@@@^@@@8          J         $+3 @G@9@8          SZ        FIRST           UF
)@@G@@  . INITIALIZE FIRST TIME THRU FLAG @F@@@9          SZ        FIRST     UG
)@@G@@        . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8          J         EXIT      UH
)@@G@@        . END OF TAPE   @G@@@8          L         A0,STIME          . CHUI
)@@G@@ECK STARTING TIME IF SPECIFIED@ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT2  @ @@@9UJ
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,CONT3  @D@@@8          L         A1,LLOGT        UK
)@@G@@  . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDATE            . COMPARE UL
)@@G@@WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60          . IF STIME MORE UM
)@@G@@THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,60*60          . IF STIMEUN
)@@G@@ MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@8          TP        A3                .   UO
)@@G@@FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZ        NBUF            UP
)@@G@@  . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  UQ
)@@G@@        . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8          JN        A2,CUR
)@@G@@ONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9          JN        A2,CUS
)@@G@@ONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9CONT3     TZ        PRIVUT
)@@G@@              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9          J         CONT4     UU
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,('EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIPUV
)@@G@@ EXEC 8 ENTRIES   @ @@@9          TNE       A0,LRUNID @ @@@9          J UW
)@@G@@        CONT2     @F@9@8CONT2     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUUX
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @F@@@9CONT4     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUUY
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @G@9@8          JZ        A0,CONT4          .    IGNORUZ
)@@G@@ING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @G@@@9          JZ        A0,CONT7          .   VA
)@@G@@ IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @^@@@8          L,U       X4,5@ @9@8CONT2AVB
)@@G@@    EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@9CONT5     EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@8      VC
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A0,'-'    @ @9@8          J         CONT3     @ @@@9      VD
)@@G@@    J         CONT6     @ @@@8          EX        TEST,X4   @ @9@8      VE
)@@G@@    J         CONT3     @ @@@9          J         CONT6     @^@9@8      VF
)@@G@@    SZ        NBUF@ @@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  @ @9@8          J VG
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @ @9@8CONT3     JGVH
)@@G@@D       X4,CONT2A @ @@@9CONT6     JGD       X4,CONT5  @F@9@8CONT4     L VI
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @F@@@9CONT7     L VJ
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          L,VK
)@@G@@H2      A0,0,A1   @F@@@8          TNZ,H1    0,X10             . CHECK IFVL
)@@G@@ TYPE TABLE INPUT @E@9@8          J         CONT4A            . NO, JUSTVM
)@@G@@ ONE TYPE   @E@@@9          J         CONT8             . NO, JUST ONE TVN
)@@G@@YPE   @F@@@8          L,H1      R1,0,X10          . SCAN TYPE TABLE FOR VO
)@@G@@MATCH @ @@@8          L         X1,0,X10  @^@@@8          LXI,U     X1,1VP
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,LTYPE  @ @@@8          SE,H2     A0,0,*X1  VQ
)@@G@@@E@9@8          J         CONT1             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @E@@@9VR
)@@G@@          J         CONT2             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@9@8      VS
)@@G@@    J         CONT5             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @F@@@9      VT
)@@G@@    J         CONT9             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @E@9@8CONT4AVU
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT5          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @E@@@9CONT8     JZVV
)@@G@@        A0,CONT9          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          TE      VW
)@@G@@  A0,LTYPE  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J       VX
)@@G@@  CONT2     @G@9@8CONT5     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEARCH KVY
)@@G@@EY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEVZ
)@@G@@ARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT6  @ @@@9      WA
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ        WDNO              . ISWB
)@@G@@ WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A            . NO, PLAIN SEARWC
)@@G@@CH KEY SPECIFIED  @G@@@9          L         X1,X5             . YES, STRWD
)@@G@@ING SEARCH SPECIFIED    @ @@@9          L,H2      X2,3,X10  @ @@@9      WE
)@@G@@    L,U       A1,24*6   @^@@@9          L,U       A2,6@A@@@9          LMWF
)@@G@@J       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@9          J         CONT2             . NOWG
)@@G@@ FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@@@9          J         CONT10            . STRING FWH
)@@G@@OUND, CONTINUE    @ @9@8          L         X4,WDNO   @ @@@9CONT9A    L WI
)@@G@@        X4,WDNO   @ @@@8          A         X4,X5     @ @@@8          L WJ
)@@G@@        A1,0,X4   @ @@@8          TE        A1,A0     @ @9@8          J WK
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @F@9@8CONT6     L,WL
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@F@@@9CONT10    L,WM
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@ @@@8          L,WN
)@@G@@U       X4,BUFF   @^@@@8          LXI,U     X4,1@ @@@8          L       WO
)@@G@@  X6,X5     @^@@@8          LXI,U     X6,1@ @@@8          BT        X4,0WP
)@@G@@,*X6  @E@@@8          S         X5,POINTER        . SAME BLOCK POINTER  WQ
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RETURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNWR
)@@G@@Z       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     WS
)@@G@@@I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FWT
)@@G@@ILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GET NEXTWU
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@9          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CWV
)@@G@@YCLE  @H@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR - FINISHED SEAWW
)@@G@@RCH (NO FIND)     @C@9@8          J         CONT1             . CONTINUEWX
)@@G@@@C@@@9          J         CONT2             . CONTINUE@F@@@8EXIT      TZWY
)@@G@@,S1     0,X10             . CHECK FOR FOR V OR FTN    @C@@@8          J WZ
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FTN     @C@@@8          J         6,X10     XA
)@@G@@        . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********************************XB
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@8. *******              RXC
)@@G@@EAD LOG ENTRY SUBROUTINE                     *******  @H@@@8. **********XD
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@8XE
)@@G@@.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ        NBUF              . ISXF
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ        ENTRYNUM          . ISXG
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J         READ3             . NOXH
)@@G@@@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YES, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESXI
)@@G@@S BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8@ @@@8READ1     S       XJ
)@@G@@  A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP             . READ NEXT 224 XK
)@@G@@WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   @C@@@8          J       XL
)@@G@@  READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INC       NBLOCKS         XM
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOP     @E@@@8          L XN
)@@G@@        A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   @ @@@8          TE      XO
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2             . NO@G@@@8      XP
)@@G@@    L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOR ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9XQ
)@@G@@          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PRESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   XR
)@@G@@@G@@@8          J         READ1             . GO BACK AND READ THAT SECTXS
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER         . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFEXT
)@@G@@RS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ           . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO XU
)@@G@@ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  @F@9@8          L,U     XV
)@@G@@  A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@F@@@9          SP1     XW
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@A@9@8          S       XX
)@@G@@  A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 @G@@@8READ3     SZ      XY
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    @F@9@8          L XZ
)@@G@@        A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @F@@@9          L YA
)@@G@@        A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @^@@@8          AUYB
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     @ @@@8          A,U     YC
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     @F@@@8          TG      YD
)@@G@@  A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    @^@@@8          SZ      YE
)@@G@@  A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9          S         A1,EYF
)@@G@@NTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @F@@@9YG
)@@G@@          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENT NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9YH
)@@G@@          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9              . RETURN  YI
)@@G@@@F@@@8READE     .                           . CLEAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   YJ
)@@G@@@E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8YK
)@@G@@          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J         EXIT              . NOYL
)@@G@@T EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$      READP             . REYM
)@@G@@AD NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3           . I/O ERROYN
)@@G@@R?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT              . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLEYO
)@@G@@ EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3        . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFEYP
)@@G@@R READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8          J         EXITYQ
)@@G@@              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          L         A0,(054160YR
)@@G@@0000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8          TE        A0,BYS
)@@G@@UFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    YT
)@@G@@@G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLEAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TAYU
)@@G@@PES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************YV
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@8. ****YW
)@@G@@******           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                 *******  YX
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************YY
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8          CSF$      FREEYZ
)@@G@@,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSF$      FREE,NFREE      ZA
)@@G@@  . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CYCLE          . IS CYCLEZB
)@@G@@ = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE          . INCREMENT LOGCZC
)@@G@@YCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'            . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9ZD
)@@G@@          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYCLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8ZE
)@@G@@          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          AN,U      A1,1            ZF
)@@G@@  . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CYCLE  @E@'@9          E$ZG
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@'@9          E$MSG   ZH
)@@G@@  USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     @A@@@'          L       ZI
)@@G@@  A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1@^@@@'          A,U     ZJ
)@@G@@  A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'          SLJ       CYCLZK
)@@G@@E             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9          E$DECV  @#@;@9      ZL
)@@G@@    E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE          . @USE MASTER,SYZM
)@@G@@S$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . @USE LOGZN
)@@G@@$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A MZO
)@@G@@ASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8ZP
)@@G@@          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9      ZQ
)@@G@@    TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANT MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    ZR
)@@G@@@B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NO@G@@@9          MSCON$  ZS
)@@G@@  MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOG FILE @E@@@9          E$ZT
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     @D@@@9          E$FD2   ZU
)@@G@@  BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9ZV
)@@G@@          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAME     @^@@@9          E$ZW
)@@G@@CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,,T3     . ABS CYCLE     ZX
)@@G@@@^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     ZY
)@@G@@@^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$DECV                    ZZ
)@@G@@  . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9          E$DAY3    BUFFAA
)@@G@@ER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9AB
)@@G@@          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1           AC
)@@G@@  . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT                     . PRINT SUAD
)@@G@@MMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   AE
)@@G@@@G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAS A START TIME SPECIFIEDAF
)@@G@@?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX             . NO@B@@@;          J AG
)@@G@@        NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,U       A5,1            AH
)@@G@@  . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,U       A6,'1'          AI
)@@G@@  .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ       CYCLE     @H@@@'      AJ
)@@G@@    JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH THAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    AK
)@@G@@@F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GET MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    AL
)@@G@@@G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COMPARE START TIME WITH CYAM
)@@G@@CLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19      .    CATALOGUE TIME   AN
)@@G@@@H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IF START TIME > CATALOGUE AO
)@@G@@TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA          .    PRESENT CYCAP
)@@G@@LE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT           .    PRESENT CYCLE    AQ
)@@G@@@F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   AR
)@@G@@@F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   AS
)@@G@@@F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   AT
)@@G@@@ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8          SZ        NBUF      AU
)@@G@@        . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRAV
)@@G@@YNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @C@9@8          J       AW
)@@G@@  1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J         1,X9            AX
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************************************AY
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@'. ******* ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBAZ
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@'. *******         BA
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@'. ****BB
)@@G@@*** INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                                     *******  BC
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX                                BD
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. *******                                             BE
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. ****************************************BF
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@'CYCLE     +         0   @E@@@'BG
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USE' IMAGE    @D@@@'      BH
)@@G@@    E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  @D@@@'          E$FD1   BI
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'          E$MSGR              BJ
)@@G@@        . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5                . REL CYCLBK
)@@G@@E     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFBL
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT      BM
)@@G@@        . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$MSG     ASG             BN
)@@G@@  . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOBO
)@@G@@G$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT ASG IMABP
)@@G@@GE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE            . RETURN  @[@@@'.     BQ
)@@G@@@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************************************BR
)@@G@@*********************** @H@@@8. *******                                 BS
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* TDATE TIME DIFFERENCBT
)@@G@@E SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@8. *******         BU
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****BV
)@@G@@*** WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77                            *******  BW
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         BX
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILL CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFBY
)@@G@@ERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONDS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPBZ
)@@G@@RESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. *******                     CA
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* INPUTS ACB
)@@G@@RE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.      *******  @H@@@8. ****CC
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  CD
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************CE
)@@G@@************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATE*   +         0         CF
)@@G@@        . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DS        A0,DTDIN        CG
)@@G@@  . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DTDIN          . CHECK IFCH
)@@G@@ MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TE,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8CI
)@@G@@          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO BAD   @F@@@8          L CJ
)@@G@@        A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATION     @ @@@8          ANCK
)@@G@@        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . ALL DONECL
)@@G@@@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964CM
)@@G@@, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP        . SAVE CONVERTED TIME CN
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8          SLJ       DTDSUB    CO
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          AN        A0,DCP
)@@G@@TDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8          L         A2,A0     CQ
)@@G@@        . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DL        A0,DTDIN        CR
)@@G@@  . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . DONE    CS
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************CT
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO SECONDS SINCE 1964      CU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************CV
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@8DTDSUB    +         0   @D@@@8CW
)@@G@@          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPUT    @^@@@8          SZCX
)@@G@@        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8CY
)@@G@@          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          AN,U      A3,1@ @@@8      CZ
)@@G@@    L         A0,A3     @E@@@8          DI,U      A2,4              . CHDA
)@@G@@ECK FOR LEAP YEARS@^@@@8          A,U       A2,1@A@@@8          MSI,U   DB
)@@G@@  A2,60*60*24     @B@@@8          MSI       A0,(60*60*24*365)     @ @@@8DC
)@@G@@          A         A0,A2     @C@@@8DTDSC1    L,S1      A2,DTDTEMP+1    DD
)@@G@@  . MONTH   @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@A@@@8DTDSC2    A         A0,DDE
)@@G@@TDTAB,A2    @ @@@8          JGD       A2,DTDSC2 @C@@@8          L,S2    DF
)@@G@@  A2,DTDTEMP+1      . DAY     @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@E@@@8      DG
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A2,60*60*24       . CONVERT TO SECS     @D@@@8          A DH
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  @G@@@8          L,S3      A3,DDI
)@@G@@TDTEMP+1       . IF LEAP YEAR AND MONTH>FEB,    @H@@@8          AND,U   DJ
)@@G@@  A3,3              .    ADD AN EXTRA DAY TO CALCULATION    @ @@@8      DK
)@@G@@    JNZ       A4,DTDSC3 @A@@@8          L,S1      A3,DTDTEMP+1    @^@@@8DL
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A3,3@ @@@8          J         DTDSC3    @A@@@8      DM
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,60*60*24     @C@@@8DTDSC3    L,H2      A2,DTDTEMP+1    DN
)@@G@@  . SECS    @D@@@8          A         A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  DO
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         *DTDSUB           . RETURN  @C@9@8DTDIN     REDP
)@@G@@S       2                 . INPUT   @C@@@9DTDIN     $RES      2         DQ
)@@G@@        . INPUT   @^@9@8DTDTEMP   RES       2   @^@@@9DTDTEMP   $RES    DR
)@@G@@  2   @^@@@8DTDTAB    +         0   @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*3DS
)@@G@@1     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*28     @A@@@8          +       DT
)@@G@@  60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8      DU
)@@G@@    +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     DV
)@@G@@@A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*6DW
)@@G@@0*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8          + DX
)@@G@@        60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @[@@@8DY
)@@G@@/.    @H@@@8. **********************************************************DZ
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@8. **********           D A T A                  EA
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@8. **********************************EB
